To implement the backend for SetYourOffer.com using Django and PostgreSQL, we will break down the task into several components. We'll focus on creating a smart authentication and registration system, an ad submission workflow, an advanced search engine, and AI features for data analysis and recommendations. We'll also integrate a GUI using a Python framework like Tkinter for demonstration purposes, although typically Django applications are web-based and don't require a separate GUI framework.

### Core Components

1. **Authentication and Registration System**
   - **Classes/Functions**:
     - `User`: Model for user data.
     - `register_user()`: Function to handle user registration.
     - `authenticate_user()`: Function to handle user login.

2. **Ad Submission Workflow**
   - **Classes/Functions**:
     - `Ad`: Model for ad data.
     - `submit_ad()`: Function to handle ad submission.

3. **Advanced Search Engine**
   - **Classes/Functions**:
     - `search_ads()`: Function to perform search queries on ads.

4. **AI Features for Data Analysis and Recommendations**
   - **Classes/Functions**:
     - `analyze_data()`: Function to perform data analysis.
     - `recommend_ads()`: Function to recommend ads based on user data.

5. **Django Views and URLs**
   - **Classes/Functions**:
     - `views.py`: Contains view functions for handling requests.
     - `urls.py`: URL routing for the application.

6. **GUI Integration (for demonstration)**
   - **Classes/Functions**:
     - `main_gui()`: Function to initialize the GUI.

#### 1. main.py

This file will serve as the entry point for the application, initializing the Django server and optionally the GUI.

FILENAME: main.py

```python
'''

Main entry point for the SetYourOffer.com backend application.

'''

import os
import django
from gui import main_gui

os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'setyouroffer.settings')
django.setup()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main_gui()
```

#### 2. models.py

This file will define the Django models for users and ads.

FILENAME: models.py

```python
'''

Defines the database models for users and ads.

'''

from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser

class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)

class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

#### 3. views.py

This file will handle HTTP requests and responses.

FILENAME: views.py

```python
'''

Handles HTTP requests for the application.

'''

from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm

def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})

def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')

def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})

def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
```

#### 4. forms.py

This file will define forms for user registration and ad submission.

FILENAME: forms.py

```python
'''

Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.

'''

from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad

class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']

class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

#### 5. urls.py

This file will define the URL routing for the application.

FILENAME: urls.py

```python
'''

Defines URL routing for the application.

'''

from django.urls import path
from . import views

urlpatterns = [
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),
]
```

#### 6. gui.py

This file will define a simple GUI using Tkinter for demonstration purposes.

FILENAME: gui.py

```python
'''

Defines a simple GUI for demonstration purposes.

'''

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox

def main_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")

    def show_message():
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")

    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)
    btn.pack(pady=20)

    root.mainloop()
```

```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.
'''
from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),
]
```

```python
import tkinter as tk

def main_gui():

    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")
    def show_message():
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")
    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)
    btn.pack(pady=20)
    root.mainloop()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for users and ads.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser
class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)
class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
```

```python  
'''  
Main entry point for the SetYourOffer.com backend application.  
'''  
import os  
import django  
from gui import main_gui

if __name__ == "__main__":
```  

models.py  
```python  
'''  
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.  
'''  
from django.db import models  
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser  

class User(AbstractUser):  
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)  

class Ad(models.Model):  
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)  
    description = models.TextField()  
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)  
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)  

class UserInteraction(models.Model):  
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'  
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)  
```  

views.py  
```python  
'''  
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.  
'''  
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect  
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout  
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction  
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm  
from .ai import generate_recommendations  

def register_user(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)  
        if form.is_valid():  
            form.save()  
            return redirect('login')  
    else:  
        form = RegistrationForm()  
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})  

def authenticate_user(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        username = request.POST['username']  
        password = request.POST['password']  
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)  
        if user is not None:  
            login(request, user)  
            return redirect('home')  
    return render(request, 'login.html')  

def submit_ad(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        form = AdForm(request.POST)  
        if form.is_valid():  
            ad = form.save(commit=False)  
            ad.user = request.user  
            ad.save()  
            return redirect('home')  
    else:  
        form = AdForm()  
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})  

def search_ads(request):  
    query = request.GET.get('q')  
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)  
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})  

def recommend_ads(request):  
    user = request.user  
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)  
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})  
```  

forms.py  
```python  
'''  
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.  
'''  
from django import forms  
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm  
from .models import User, Ad  

class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):  
    class Meta:  
        model = User  
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']  

class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):  
    class Meta:  
        model = Ad  
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']  
```

```python  
urlpatterns = [

    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),  
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),  
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),  
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),  
]
```  

ai.py  
```python  
'''  
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.  
'''  
import numpy as np  
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity  
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad  

def generate_recommendations(user):  
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)  
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]  
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)  

    # Example: Simple content-based filtering using ad descriptions  
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]  
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]  

    user_vector = np.mean([np.array([ord(char) for char in desc]) for desc in user_interactions], axis=0)  
    ad_vectors = [np.array([ord(char) for char in desc]) for desc in ad_descriptions]  

    similarities = cosine_similarity([user_vector], ad_vectors)[0]  
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]  

    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]  
```

 main.py  
```python  
'''  
Main entry point for the SetYourOffer.com backend application.  
'''  
import os  
import django  
from gui import main_gui  
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'setyouroffer.settings')  
django.setup()  
if __name__ == "__main__":  
    main_gui()  
```  

models.py  
```python  
'''  
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.  
'''  
from django.db import models  
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser  

class User(AbstractUser):  
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)  

class Ad(models.Model):  
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)  
    description = models.TextField()  
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)  
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)  

class UserInteraction(models.Model):  
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'  
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)  
```  

views.py  
```python  
'''  
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.  
'''  
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect  
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout  
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction  
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm  
from .ai import generate_recommendations  

def register_user(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)  
        if form.is_valid():  
            form.save()  
            return redirect('login')  
    else:  
        form = RegistrationForm()  
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})  

def authenticate_user(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        username = request.POST['username']  
        password = request.POST['password']  
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)  
        if user is not None:  
            login(request, user)  
            return redirect('home')  
    return render(request, 'login.html')  

def submit_ad(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        form = AdForm(request.POST)  
        if form.is_valid():  
            ad = form.save(commit=False)  
            ad.user = request.user  
            ad.save()  
            return redirect('home')  
    else:  
        form = AdForm()  
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})  

def search_ads(request):  
    query = request.GET.get('q')  
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)  
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})  

def recommend_ads(request):  
    user = request.user  
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)  
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})  
```  

forms.py  
```python  
'''  
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.  
'''  
from django import forms  
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm  
from .models import User, Ad  

class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):  
    class Meta:  
        model = User  
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']  

class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):  
    class Meta:  
        model = Ad  
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']  
```  

urls.py  
```python  
'''  
Defines URL routing for the application.  
'''  
from django.urls import path  
from . import views  

urlpatterns = [  
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),  
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),  
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),  
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),  
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),  
]  
```

```python  
import numpy as np  
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity

def generate_recommendations(user):
```  

```python
Main entry point for the SetYourOffer.com backend application.
```

models.py
```python
'''  
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.  
'''  
from django.db import models  
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser  
class User(AbstractUser):  
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)  
class Ad(models.Model):  
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)  
    description = models.TextField()  
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)  
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)  
class UserInteraction(models.Model):  
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'  
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)  
```

views.py
```python
'''  
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.  
'''  
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect  
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout  
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction  
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm  
from .ai import generate_recommendations  
def register_user(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)  
        if form.is_valid():  
            form.save()  
            return redirect('login')  
    else:  
        form = RegistrationForm()  
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})  
def authenticate_user(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        username = request.POST['username']  
        password = request.POST['password']  
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)  
        if user is not None:  
            login(request, user)  
            return redirect('home')  
    return render(request, 'login.html')  
def submit_ad(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        form = AdForm(request.POST)  
        if form.is_valid():  
            ad = form.save(commit=False)  
            ad.user = request.user  
            ad.save()  
            return redirect('home')  
    else:  
        form = AdForm()  
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})  
def search_ads(request):  
    query = request.GET.get('q')  
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)  
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})  
def recommend_ads(request):  
    user = request.user  
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)  
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})  
```

forms.py
```python
'''  
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.  
'''  
from django import forms  
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm  
from .models import User, Ad  
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):  
    class Meta:  
        model = User  
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']  
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):  
    class Meta:  
        model = Ad  
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']  
```

```python
'''  
Defines URL routing for the application.  
'''  
from django.urls import path  
from . import views  
urlpatterns = [  
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),  
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),  
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),  
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),  
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),  
]
```

```python
def main_gui():  
    root = tk.Tk()  
    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")  
    def show_message():  
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")  
    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)  
    btn.pack(pady=20)  
    root.mainloop()  
```

ai.py
```python
'''  
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.  
'''  
import numpy as np  
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity  
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad  
def generate_recommendations(user):  
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)  
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]  
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)  
    # Example: Simple content-based filtering using ad descriptions  
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]  
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]  
    user_vector = np.mean([np.array([ord(char) for char in desc]) for desc in user_interactions], axis=0)  
    ad_vectors = [np.array([ord(char) for char in desc]) for desc in ad_descriptions]  
    similarities = cosine_similarity([user_vector], ad_vectors)[0]  
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]  
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]  
```

The highest priority issue in the provided code is the use of a simple content-based filtering method in the `generate_recommendations` function within `ai.py`. This approach uses ASCII values of characters in ad descriptions to generate vectors, which is not an effective or meaningful way to represent text data for similarity calculations. This could lead to poor recommendation quality.

**Suggestion for Revision:**
1. Replace the current vectorization method with a more sophisticated text representation technique, such as TF-IDF (Term Frequency-Inverse Document Frequency) or word embeddings (e.g., using libraries like `gensim` or `spaCy`).
2. Update the `generate_recommendations` function to use the new representation for calculating similarities.

Here's a brief example using TF-IDF:

```python
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer

def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

This change will improve the quality of recommendations by using a more meaningful representation of text data.

This approach uses ASCII values of characters in ad descriptions to generate vectors, which is not an effective or meaningful way to represent text data for similarity calculations. **Suggestion for Revision:**

Here's a brief example using TF-IDF:

```python
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer

def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

This change will improve the quality of recommendations by using a more meaningful representation of text data.

models.py
```python
'''  
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.  
'''  
from django.db import models  
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser  
class User(AbstractUser):  
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)  
class Ad(models.Model):  
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)  
    description = models.TextField()  
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)  
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)  
class UserInteraction(models.Model):  
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)  
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'  
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)  
```

views.py
```python
'''  
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.  
'''  
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect  
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout  
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction  
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm  
from .ai import generate_recommendations  
def register_user(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)  
        if form.is_valid():  
            form.save()  
            return redirect('login')  
    else:  
        form = RegistrationForm()  
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})  
def authenticate_user(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        username = request.POST['username']  
        password = request.POST['password']  
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)  
        if user is not None:  
            login(request, user)  
            return redirect('home')  
    return render(request, 'login.html')  
def submit_ad(request):  
    if request.method == 'POST':  
        form = AdForm(request.POST)  
        if form.is_valid():  
            ad = form.save(commit=False)  
            ad.user = request.user  
            ad.save()  
            return redirect('home')  
    else:  
        form = AdForm()  
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})  
def search_ads(request):  
    query = request.GET.get('q')  
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)  
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})  
def recommend_ads(request):  
    user = request.user  
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)  
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})  
```

forms.py
```python
'''  
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.  
'''  
from django import forms  
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm  
from .models import User, Ad  
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):  
    class Meta:  
        model = User  
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']  
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):  
    class Meta:  
        model = Ad  
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']  
```

```python
'''  
Defines URL routing for the application.  
'''  
from django.urls import path  
from . import views  
urlpatterns = [  
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),  
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),  
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),  
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),  
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),  
]
```

```python
def main_gui():  
    root = tk.Tk()  
    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")  
    def show_message():  
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")  
    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)  
    btn.pack(pady=20)  
    root.mainloop()
```

ai.py
```python
'''  
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.  
'''  
import numpy as np  
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity  
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad  
def generate_recommendations(user):  
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)  
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]  
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)  
    # Example: Simple content-based filtering using ad descriptions  
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]  
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]  
    user_vector = np.mean([np.array([ord(char) for char in desc]) for desc in user_interactions], axis=0)  
    ad_vectors = [np.array([ord(char) for char in desc]) for desc in ad_descriptions]  
    similarities = cosine_similarity([user_vector], ad_vectors)[0]  
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]  
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]  
```

"
Comments on Codes:
"The highest priority issue in the provided code is the use of a simple content-based filtering method in the `generate_recommendations` function within `ai.py`. This approach uses ASCII values of characters in ad descriptions to generate vectors, which is not an effective or meaningful way to represent text data for similarity calculations. This could lead to poor recommendation quality.

**Suggestion for Revision:**
1. Replace the current vectorization method with a more sophisticated text representation technique, such as TF-IDF (Term Frequency-Inverse Document Frequency) or word embeddings (e.g., using libraries like `gensim` or `spaCy`).
2. Update the `generate_recommendations` function to use the new representation for calculating similarities.

Here's a brief example using TF-IDF:

```python
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer

def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

This change will improve the quality of recommendations by using a more meaningful representation of text data."

```python
'''
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser

class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)

class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)

class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations

def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})

def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')

def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})

def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})

def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```

ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad

def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

```python
'''
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser

class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)

class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)

class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

```python
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad

def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)

    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]

    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser
class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)
class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.
'''
from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),
]
```

```python
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def main_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")
    def show_message():
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")
    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)
    btn.pack(pady=20)
    root.mainloop()
```

ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad
def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser
class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)
class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.
'''
from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),
]
```

```python
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")
    def show_message():
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")
    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)
    btn.pack(pady=20)
    root.mainloop()
```

ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad
def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

```python
'''
```
```python
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser

class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)

class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)

class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations

def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})

def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')

def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})

def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})

def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.
'''
from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad

class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']

class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views

urlpatterns = [
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),
]
```

ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad

def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

```python
'''
```
```python
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.
'''
from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),
]
```

```python
'''
Defines a simple GUI for demonstration purposes.

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def main_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")
    def show_message():
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")
    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)
    btn.pack(pady=20)
    root.mainloop()
```

ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad
def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main entry point for the SetYourOffer.com backend application.
'''
import os
import django
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'setyouroffer.settings')
django.setup()
# If running the server directly from this script is desired, uncomment the following lines:
# from django.core.management import execute_from_command_line
# import sys
# execute_from_command_line(sys.argv)
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser
class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)
class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.
'''
from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the application.

from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),
]
```

```python
import tkinter as tk

def main_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")
    def show_message():
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")
    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)
    btn.pack(pady=20)
    root.mainloop()
```

ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad
def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

```python
'''
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser
class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)
class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.
'''
from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

```python
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
```

ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad
def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

```python
'''
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser
class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)
class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```

ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad
def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

```python
Main entry point for the SetYourOffer.com backend application.
'''
import os
import django
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'setyouroffer.settings')
django.setup()
```

models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser
class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)
class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```
views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```
forms.py
```python
'''
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.
'''
from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),
]
```

```python
'''
Defines a simple GUI for demonstration purposes.
'''
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def main_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")
    def show_message():
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")
    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)
    btn.pack(pady=20)
    root.mainloop()
```
ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad
def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```

```python
'''
Main entry point for the SetYourOffer.com backend application.
'''
import os
import django
os.environ.setdefault('DJANGO_SETTINGS_MODULE', 'setyouroffer.settings')
django.setup()
```
