models.py
```python
'''
Defines the database models for users, ads, and AI-related data.
'''
from django.db import models
from django.contrib.auth.models import AbstractUser
class User(AbstractUser):
    email = models.EmailField(unique=True)
class Ad(models.Model):
    title = models.CharField(max_length=255)
    description = models.TextField()
    price = models.DecimalField(max_digits=10, decimal_places=2)
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
class UserInteraction(models.Model):
    user = models.ForeignKey(User, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    ad = models.ForeignKey(Ad, on_delete=models.CASCADE)
    interaction_type = models.CharField(max_length=50)  # e.g., 'view', 'click', 'favorite'
    timestamp = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True)
```

views.py
```python
'''
Handles HTTP requests for the application, including AI-based recommendations.
'''
from django.shortcuts import render, redirect
from django.contrib.auth import authenticate, login, logout
from .models import User, Ad, UserInteraction
from .forms import RegistrationForm, AdForm
from .ai import generate_recommendations
def register_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = RegistrationForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            form.save()
            return redirect('login')
    else:
        form = RegistrationForm()
    return render(request, 'register.html', {'form': form})
def authenticate_user(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        username = request.POST['username']
        password = request.POST['password']
        user = authenticate(request, username=username, password=password)
        if user is not None:
            login(request, user)
            return redirect('home')
    return render(request, 'login.html')
def submit_ad(request):
    if request.method == 'POST':
        form = AdForm(request.POST)
        if form.is_valid():
            ad = form.save(commit=False)
            ad.user = request.user
            ad.save()
            return redirect('home')
    else:
        form = AdForm()
    return render(request, 'submit_ad.html', {'form': form})
def search_ads(request):
    query = request.GET.get('q')
    ads = Ad.objects.filter(title__icontains=query)
    return render(request, 'search_results.html', {'ads': ads})
def recommend_ads(request):
    user = request.user
    recommendations = generate_recommendations(user)
    return render(request, 'recommendations.html', {'recommendations': recommendations})
```

forms.py
```python
'''
Defines forms for user registration and ad submission.
'''
from django import forms
from django.contrib.auth.forms import UserCreationForm
from .models import User, Ad
class RegistrationForm(UserCreationForm):
    class Meta:
        model = User
        fields = ['username', 'email', 'password1', 'password2']
class AdForm(forms.ModelForm):
    class Meta:
        model = Ad
        fields = ['title', 'description', 'price']
```

urls.py
```python
'''
Defines URL routing for the application.
'''
from django.urls import path
from . import views
urlpatterns = [
    path('register/', views.register_user, name='register'),
    path('login/', views.authenticate_user, name='login'),
    path('submit_ad/', views.submit_ad, name='submit_ad'),
    path('search/', views.search_ads, name='search_ads'),
    path('recommendations/', views.recommend_ads, name='recommendations'),
]
```

```python
'''
Defines a simple GUI for demonstration purposes.

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
def main_gui():
    root = tk.Tk()
    root.title("SetYourOffer.com Backend")
    def show_message():
        messagebox.showinfo("Info", "This is a demonstration GUI for the backend.")
    btn = tk.Button(root, text="Show Info", command=show_message)
    btn.pack(pady=20)
    root.mainloop()
```

ai.py
```python
'''
Defines AI-related functionality for data analysis and recommendations.
'''
import numpy as np
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from .models import UserInteraction, Ad
def generate_recommendations(user):
    interactions = UserInteraction.objects.filter(user=user)
    ad_ids = [interaction.ad.id for interaction in interactions]
    ads = Ad.objects.exclude(id__in=ad_ids)
    user_interactions = [interaction.ad.description for interaction in interactions]
    ad_descriptions = [ad.description for ad in ads]
    # Use TF-IDF to vectorize the descriptions
    vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
    all_descriptions = user_interactions + ad_descriptions
    tfidf_matrix = vectorizer.fit_transform(all_descriptions)
    user_vector = tfidf_matrix[:len(user_interactions)].mean(axis=0)
    ad_vectors = tfidf_matrix[len(user_interactions):]
    similarities = cosine_similarity(user_vector, ad_vectors)[0]
    recommended_ads = sorted(zip(ads, similarities), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]
    return [ad for ad, _ in recommended_ads]
```
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

Please fill out this form and we'll set up a dedicated support Slack channel.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

## 📖 Documentation

Please see [here](https://python.langchain.com) for full documentation on:

- Getting started (installation, setting up the environment, simple examples)

- How-To examples (demos, integrations, helper functions)

- Reference (full API docs)

- Resources (high-level explanation of core concepts)
```

# SetYourOffer.com Backend User Manual

Welcome to the SetYourOffer.com backend application! This software is designed to provide a robust backend system for managing user authentication, ad submissions, advanced search capabilities, and AI-driven recommendations. The application is built using Django and PostgreSQL, ensuring a scalable and reliable infrastructure.

## Main Functions

### 1. Smart Authentication and Registration System
- **User Registration**: Allows new users to create an account with a unique email and password.
- **User Authentication**: Enables users to log in securely using their credentials.

### 2. Ad Submission Workflow
- **Submit Ads**: Users can submit advertisements with details such as title, description, and price.
- **Manage Ads**: Users can view and manage their submitted ads.

### 3. Advanced Search Engine
- **Search Ads**: Users can search for ads using keywords, with results filtered based on relevance.

### 4. AI Features for Data Analysis and Recommendations
- **AI Recommendations**: Provides personalized ad recommendations based on user interactions and preferences.

## Installation

### Prerequisites
- Python 3.8 or higher
- PostgreSQL
- Django

### Environment Setup

1. **Clone the Repository**
   ```bash
   git clone https://github.com/yourusername/setyouroffer-backend.git
   cd setyouroffer-backend
   ```

2. **Create a Virtual Environment**
   ```bash
   python -m venv venv
   source venv/bin/activate  # On Windows use `venv\Scripts\activate`
   ```

3. **Install Dependencies**
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

4. **Configure Database**
   - Ensure PostgreSQL is installed and running.
   - Create a new database for the application.
   - Update the `DATABASES` setting in `setyouroffer/settings.py` with your database credentials.

5. **Apply Migrations**
   ```bash
   python manage.py migrate
   ```

6. **Run the Server**
   ```bash
   python manage.py runserver
   ```

## Usage

### Accessing the Application

- Open your web browser and navigate to `http://localhost:8000` to access the application.

### User Registration and Login

- **Register**: Go to `/register/` to create a new account.
- **Login**: Go to `/login/` to log in with your credentials.

### Submitting and Managing Ads

- **Submit Ad**: Navigate to `/submit_ad/` to create a new advertisement.
- **Search Ads**: Use the search bar on the homepage to find ads by keywords.
- **Recommendations**: Visit `/recommendations/` to view personalized ad recommendations.

## AI Features

- The AI module uses TF-IDF and cosine similarity to analyze user interactions and provide recommendations.
- Recommendations are dynamically generated based on user behavior and ad content.

## Support

For any issues or questions, please contact our support team at support@setyouroffer.com.

Thank you for using SetYourOffer.com backend application! We hope it meets your needs and enhances your digital experience.

2. **Create a Virtual Environment**
   ```bash
   python -m venv venv
   source venv/bin/activate  # On Windows use `venv\Scripts\activate`
   ```

3. **Install Dependencies**
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

4. **Configure Database**
   - Ensure PostgreSQL is installed and running.
   - Create a new database for the application.
   - Update the `DATABASES` setting in `setyouroffer/settings.py` with your database credentials.

5. **Apply Migrations**
   ```bash
   python manage.py migrate
   ```

6. **Run the Server**
   ```bash
   python manage.py runserver
   ```

## Usage

### Accessing the Application

- Open your web browser and navigate to `http://localhost:8000` to access the application.

### User Registration and Login

- **Register**: Go to `/register/` to create a new account.
- **Login**: Go to `/login/` to log in with your credentials.

### Submitting and Managing Ads

- **Submit Ad**: Navigate to `/submit_ad/` to create a new advertisement.
- **Search Ads**: Use the search bar on the homepage to find ads by keywords.
- **Recommendations**: Visit `/recommendations/` to view personalized ad recommendations.

## AI Features

- The AI module uses TF-IDF and cosine similarity to analyze user interactions and provide recommendations.
- Recommendations are dynamically generated based on user behavior and ad content.

## Support

For any issues or questions, please contact our support team at support@setyouroffer.com.
